No group/channel support, no inline permission buttons, no streaming preview. Permissions use text <code>/perm ...</code> commands. Image inbound only (no image replies).</p>\n</blockquote>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Go to <a href=\"https://q.qq.com/qqbot/openclaw\" rel=\"nofollow\">QQ Bot OpenClaw</a></li>\n<li>Create a QQ Bot or select an existing one → get <strong>App ID</strong> and <strong>App Secret</strong> (only two required fields)</li>\n<li>Configure sandbox access and scan QR code with QQ to add the bot</li>\n<li><code>CTI_QQ_ALLOWED_USERS</code> takes <code>user_openid</code> values (not QQ numbers) — can be left empty initially</li>\n<li>Set <code>CTI_QQ_IMAGE_ENABLED=false</code> if the underlying provider doesn't support image input</li>\n</ol>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">WeChat / Weixin</h3><a id=\"user-content-wechat--weixin\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: WeChat / Weixin\" href=\"#wechat--weixin\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">WeChat currently uses QR login, single-account mode, text-based permissions, and no streaming preview.</p>\n</blockquote>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Run the local QR helper from your installed skill directory:\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Claude Code default install: <code>cd ~/.claude/skills/claude-to-im &amp;&amp; npm run weixin:login</code></li>\n<li>Codex default install: <code>cd ~/.codex/skills/claude-to-im &amp;&amp; npm run weixin:login</code></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li>The helper writes <code>~/.claude-to-im/runtime/weixin-login.html</code> and tries to open it in your browser automatically</li>\n<li>Scan the QR code with WeChat and confirm on your phone</li>\n<li>On success, the linked account is stored in <code>~/.claude-to-im/data/weixin-accounts.json</code></li>\n<li>Running the helper again replaces the previously linked WeChat account</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Additional notes:</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><code>CTI_WEIXIN_MEDIA_ENABLED</code> controls inbound image/file/video downloads only</li>\n<li>Voice messages only use WeChat's own built-in speech-to-text text</li>\n<li>If WeChat does not provide <code>voice_item.text</code>, the bridge replies with an error instead of downloading/transcribing raw voice audio</li>\n<li>Permission approvals use text <code>/perm ...</code> commands or quick <code>1/2/3</code> replies</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\"
